O vos, tres chiers filz, je vos ai acomplit cest livre qui est li derriens de la science de medicine ensamble l’emplissement de lui, et ai fait la fin per ses expositions et par ses declarations.	You, three sons, I have fulfilled this book that is behind the science of medicine the fulfillment of it, and have ended for its exposures and by its declarations.
Et m’est venu en vision que je le vos acomplisse avec cest traitier, qui est partie de l’uevre de mains, c’est a savoir «cyrurgie».	And it came to my vision that I have completed this with the method, which is from the work of hands, it is to say "surgery".
Et por ceu que l’uevre de mains est fortraite en nostre region et est etraingie dou tout en tout, si est perie li science et decopee, et n’est riens demorez de li fuers que les petites descriptions en livres des anciens que les mains ont muees.	And because the work of hands is forbidden in our region and is despised in every way, if it is perished by the science and practice, and there is nothing left of the works but the small descriptions in books that the hands have moved.
Et de ceu est venue li error et li vanitez, et sont closes les ententions et est aloignie li science.	And this is how the error and vanity have come about, and the intentions are closed and science is alienated.
Or me semble que je la vuel vivifier ensamble l’ordination de cest traitier selonc la voie d’exposition et de declaration et de l’abreviation; et venrai ensamble les formes des ferremens de cautere, et des autres estrumens de l’uevre avec l’ajostement de la declaration et de preparation de li, sicom il est mestier.	I seem to think that I will revive this ordination of this cauterization according to the way of exposure and declaration and abbreviation; and I will bring together the forms of the instruments of cauterization and other instruments of the work with the alignment of the declaration and preparation of it, as it is their craft.
Et por la raison de ceu que nuls boins maistres de mains n’est trovez en nostre tens, est li ars de medicine eslongié.	And because no skilled hands masters are found in our time, the art of medicine is elongated.
Et covient celui qui s’en entremet sormonter en la science d’anathomie, si com Galiens dit, tant qu’il saiche la juement des menbres, et les formes et les conjunctions et les separations d’aus, et aient connissance des osses et des nerf et des brais et le nombre d’ous, et le demenement et des voines movans et des reposans, et dou leu de lor issue.	And it is necessary for him who enters this field to surpass in the science of anatomy, as Galen says, so that he knows the judgment of the members, and their forms and conjunctions and separations of parts, and has knowledge of the bones, nerves, bones, and teeth, and the number of joints, and the brain and the movable and resting joints, and also the issue of the same.
Et por ceu dist Ypocras que li nons avec le non est mout, et avec l’uevre est poc; et meismement en l’art de main.	And for this reason, Iophras says that the non with the non is not enough, and with the will is little; and at the same time in the art of the hand.
Nos vos disons en l’introite de cest livre que qui n’est conissans des choses devant dites, si se gart qu’il ne chiece en error et qu’il n’ocie les homes; ensi que j’ai veut maintes fois plusors de ces qui s’entremettent de ceste science et si s’abandonent sen science et sens experiment.	In the introduction of this book, we say that who are not acquainted with things said, if they try it, they may err and harm men; and I have often seen these who enter into this science and abandon the science and sense of experience.
Car je vis un fol mire qui copa I apostume de scrophules ou col d’une femme, et copa les arteres dou col; por coi tant de sanc issit hors que li femme cheit morte entre ses mains.	For I see a madman who cuts off my apostile from scrophules or the col of a woman, and cuts the arteries of the col; because so much blood issues outside that the woman died in her hands.
Et vis I autre mire qui traït une piere d’un home d’eaige, et li piere estoit grans; si emporta avec li une piece de la vessie, et fut mors li hons dedens III jors.	And see if another mirror that treats a piercing of a man's ear, and the piercing was large; if it is removed with the piece of the bladder, and he died in the third year.
Et je i avoie ja esteit apelez por lou traire, et vis la disposition dou malaide et la grandor de la piere, et soi bien s’on lou tailloit il en morroit.	I had already been called to treat, and see the position of the surgeon and the size of the piercing, and if it was well cut, it died.
Et vis I autre mire qui prist en cure I duc de nostre terre qui avoit la jambe brisie, et avec la briseure ot plaie; et li mires plains d’ignorance estraint la brisure sus la plaie as esteles par fort lieure, et ne lassa a la plaie point de xalain, et le lassa ensi I termine; et li comanda qu’il ne la desliast mie; et demora ensi que li jambe fut toute enflee et li piez et vint a perdition.	And see if another mirror that treated the leg of our king who had a broken bone, and with the fracture it was plated; and the surgeon's ignorance forced the fracture on the plate as it was done in a short time, and did not leave any pain in the plate, and left it finally; and he commanded that it should not be dislodged; and later that the leg became completely swollen and the bone and came to destruction.
Je fuis apelez por venir a lui, et me hastai por venir deslier la jambe; et quant je l’oi desloie si fut em pais et ne sentit point de dolor.	I am summoned to come to him, and I hurried to come and cut off the leg; and when I saw it dislocated if it was in pain and did not feel any pain.
Mais toute voie li corruptions estoit ja confermee ou membre, et ne la poi saner; et ne cessa li corrution d’aler par le membre tant que li membres fut dou tout perdus.	But all paths of the corruption were already confirmed by the member, and it could not be healed; and the corruption continued to spread through the member as long as the member was completely lost.
Et vis I autre mire qui effondra I apostume enchancreit, et puis enflama per le malice de sa signorie.	And see another mirror that will fall and be enchanted, and then burned through the malice of his lordship.
Car chancre, quant il est purs d’umor melancolique, ne covient mie qu’on i(l) touche de fer s’il n’est en teil leu c’on puisse toute oster ce que est corrumpus.	For gangrene, when it is free of melancholic humor, only one thing is needed if it is not in its entirety the leg that can be healed completely what is corrupted.
Et por ceu, treschier filz, vos est besoig que vos sachiez que oevre de mains est devisee en II divisions: c’est asavoir, huevre ou il a peril en plusors dispositions; et je mostrerai en chescun leu de cest livre ou il a paour et peril.	1. Therefore, thrice-worn threads, you should be glad to know that the work of hands is divided into two sections: this is knowledge, whether it is safe in other arrangements; and I will show you in each chapter of this book where there is danger and risk.
Por coi il est besoig que vos vos en gardez, si que li fol mire ne puissent mal parler de vos Si prenez vos armes en cusenson, et entreprenez vos malaides legierement et fermement, et usez de la millor voie si que per la graice de Deu vos venez a salut et soiez loez; et lassiez les maladies espoantables de grief saniteit; et ostez vos armes de ceu que vos fait douter, et aiez foit en vos si que vos puissiez venir de cestui monde a l’autre de gloire.	2. Therefore, take care of your threads so that they may not be harmed by others' words; if you take up your weapons in anger, and use your remedies lightly but firmly, and choose the better way for the grace of God, so that you may come to salvation and be healthy; and leave the unwholesome diseases of grief behind; and keep your weapons ready in case you have to come from this world to another for glory.
Galiens dist en aucuns de ses amonestemens: «Ne prenez mie en cure male maladie, que vos ne soiez apelez fol mire.	Galen's disciples often ignored his advice: "Do not take half-measures in the treatment of disease, lest you be called a foolish man.
» J’ai deviseit cest traitier selonc III chapitres.	I have seen this treatise in three chapters.
Li premiers chapitres est des cauteres de feu et dé cauteres de medicine ague, et est li chapitres ordenez de lou chief jusques as piez; et des formes des estrumens, et des ferremens de cautere, et de tout ceu qui est necessaire en l’ueuvre.	The first chapter is about fire cauterization and medicinal cauterization, and it is arranged in order from the head down to the feet; as well as the forms of strangulation, and the making of cauterizing irons, and all that is necessary in the work.
Li secons chapitres si est de taillier et de percier, et des ventouses et des plaies, et des estractions des saiettes, et des semblans choses; et est li chapitres ordenez et les formes des estrumens.	The second chapter is about cutting and piercing, and ventouses and wounds, and the extraction of arrows, and similar things; and it is arranged in order and the forms of strangulation.
Li tiers chapitres est de restorer les dislocations et des torcions, et des semblans choses; et est ordeneiz des lou chief jusc’as piez, et des formes des estrumens.	The third chapter is about restoring dislocations and twists, and similar things; and it is ordered by the chief surgeons, and the forms of the splints.
Ainsois que nos nos remembriens de l’uevre, il covient que je die la qualiteit de l’aide et dou nuisement de chescune complexion.	However, if we remember our work, it is necessary to mention the quality of the help and not each complexion.
Je dis que li qualiteis de l’aide, et dou nuisement, est li plus longe parole et subtilz science et li secrez reponus; et de ceu parlerent li plusors des saiges, et s’acorderent a ceu; et me soffisent poc lor paroles, car je redous la longesce.	I say that the quality of the help, and not each complexion, is the longest word and the most subtle science and the secret remedy; and for this they speak of more cases, and agree to this; and they are few in their words because I doubt the longevity.
Je dis que cautere aide universement a toute complexion ou il a matiere, fuer que II complexions: c’est a savoir complexion chaude sens matere, et complexion seche sens matere.	I say that cauterization helps universally with all complexions or matters, for which complexions: it is to know hot complexions with matter, and dry complexions with matter.
En complexion chaude et seche ensamble matiere, deviserent aucun et dirent que cautere i est grans aide; et li autre dirent le contraire: que cautere ne vaut a maladie que vient de chalor et de sechour.	In hot and dry complexions, none will devise or say that cauterization is great help; and the other will say the opposite: that cauterization is only good for disease that comes from choler and dryness.
Car li nature dou feu si est chaude, et ne doit mie estre cureiz de chaude maladie par chalor, ne per sechour; et dist cil qui dist lou contraire que cautere fait grant aide a maladie chaude et seche que vient en cors des homes.	For the nature of fire is hot, and should not be cured for hot disease by choler, nor by dryness; and that is what he who says the opposite says, that cauterization helps great with hot disease that comes from the hearts of men.
Car quant tu comperes le cors de l’ome et sa moistor a la complexion dou feu, tu trueves le cors froit.	For when you perceive the chest of the patient and its moisture at the complexion of hot fire, you should immediately close the wound.
Et je m’acorde a ceste parole.	And I agree with this word.
Car je l’ai troveit aucune fois per experiment.	For I have never found it at any time by experience.
Et toute voie, ne s’en entremette mie fuers que cil qui l’a esproveit, et qui conoit par lonc usaige le chapistre des cauteres, et la diversiteit des complexions des homes, et les dispositions et les causes de lor maladies, et les sorvenues et l’espaice dou tens; des autres complexions n’avons nos mie paour, meismement em maladies froides et moistes.	And all ways, it does not interfere more than he who has experienced it, and knows by long use of the cauterization chapter, and the diversity of complexions of men, and their dispositions and causes of their diseases, and their symptoms and their spaciousness; others complexions have no fear for us, but rather in cold and moist diseases.
Et tuit li mire s’asemblerent et s’acorderent au cautere.	And then they resemble and agree with the cauterization.
Et sachiez, filz, que cautere ensamble feu si est des secrez des cures, et de plus grant bonteit que cautere de medicine ardant.	Understand, children, that cauterization is similar to fire if it contains the secrets of remedies, and more beneficial than cauterization with hot medicine.
Car li feus est simples, et ne vient mie fuers que au membre qui est cuis, et ne nuit a autre membre se poc nom.	For the fire is simple, and only comes to harm when it reaches the member that is cooked, and does not harm other members.
Les medicines ardans vienent de membre a autre en aloignant, et font venir au membre maladies de grief sanation; et par aventure ocit lou malaide Li feus por sa hautece et por la bonteit de sa substance ne fait mie ceu, s’il n’i a superfluiteit.	Hot remedies come from one part of the body to another by allaying, and bring about the cure of the member in need; and sometimes the patient Li feus por his high quality and the goodness of his substance does not harm, if he has no superfluity.
Et ceu vos ai je troveit par experiment et par la longesce dou servise et de l’estude que j’ai mis en l’art, et esteit sus la verteit des choses; et por ceu je m’escuse de la longesce de la parole, car il ne me plait mie que je vos oste le secreit qui est reponus ou feu, et la qualiteit de l’uevre, coment il deboute les maladies des cors, si com li philosophe le dit en demostrant; or le recevez en vos pensees.	1. And I found this in my research through experiment and the length of service and the study I have given to this art, and it is true; and for this I apologize for the length of the language, because I only want to share with you the secret that is fire or water, and the quality of the work, as it affects the diseases of the body, just as the philosopher says by demonstrating; and receive it in your thoughts.
Et sachiez, fil, que il s’acorderent en quel tens doient estre faites les cauteres, et eslirent prientens.	1. Know, boy, that the cauteries should be made with proper tension and not too tight.
Et je dis que cautere est covenable en tous tens, por ceu que li nuisemens sorvenans est desoz mis par l’aide dou cautere; et meismement se li cauteres est por dolors necessaires fors et hastans que ne puent atendre le tens que plus grans malice ne veigne au membre.	1. I say that cauterization is useful in all tensions because the pain of the wound is not well managed by the aid of the cauterization; and I also say that if the cauterization is for necessary pains, it should be done with the smallest tension that does not cause great harm to the member.
Et n’i pensez onques, chier fil, si com font li fol mire; car a la maladie qui est sanee par cautere n’a point de revenue; et il le dient ensi; mais il n’est mie si com il cuident, por ce que cauteres nen est que medicine qui mue la complexion, et seche les humors que sont cause de la dolor, et vaut mues que medicine por le hastement de sa valor, et por la vertut de son oevre et de sa signorie.	And never think, chief, that the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return; for the disease that is cured by cauterization has no return; and he says thus, but it is not so if one takes care, because cauterization is only a medicine that dries the complexion, and dries the humors that cause pain, and is valued as a medicine to hasten one's valor, and for one's virtue in one's work and signory.
Et possans chose est que li maladie viegne aucune fois selonc la complexion dou malaide et lou leu de la maladie et sa vertut; et sont assemblees en lui les superfluitez par l’aquisition des viandes et des semblans choses, se ce n’est cauteres administrez em leu ou il ait poc de superfluitez et de moistor, si com cauteres de dens por la dolor, et les semblans choses, et teil dolor ne revient mie; mais ce avient poc.	And it is possible that the disease does not return at all according to the complexion of the patient and the lesion of the disease and its virtue; and they are assembled in him by the acquisition of meat and the superfluities, unless cauterization is administered to him or he has little acquisition and moisture, as for cauterization for pain, and the superfluities, and only part of the pain does not return; but this is rare.
Et mout de gens n’entendent mie por coi cauteres est apelez li derriens de medecine, et c’est voir; mais il ne croient mie que cauteres vaille aprés medicine, mais lor ententions est fause, et est cauteres li derriens de medicine por ceu que quant nos aministrons manieres de cures en aucune maladie et elles ne valent, adonc administrons nos le cautere, et il vaut.	1. And many people do not understand why cauterization is called surgery by others, and this is seen; but they only believe that cauterization is after medicine, but we understand it is false, and cauterization is surgery because when we administer remedies for any disease and they do not work, we then use cauterization, and it works.
Adonques apert bien que cauteres est li derriens de medicine, ne mie selonc l’entention des folz mires.	2. Therefore, it is well that cauterization is called surgery, but not according to the attention of the ignorant.
Li ancien dirent que cauteres d’estrument d’or est muedres que de fer, et ne dirent ceu fuers que por la qualiteit de l’or et por la hautece de sa substance; et dirent que li leus de cautere ne fait mie porriture, mais ceu n’est mie voir car je l’ai esprovei, et ai troveit que c’est voir en aucuns homes; et cauteres d’or vaut mues que de fer, si com il lou dirent.	3. The ancients said that a gold cauterization instrument was as harmful as one made of iron, and they said this because of the quality of the gold and the highness of its substance; and they said that the gold cautery did not cause any poisoning, but it is true because I have experienced it, and I found that it is true in some men; and the gold cauterization is as good as iron, as they say.
Et toutevoie quant tu chaufes estrument d’or, tu ne seis mie quant il est chaus par la color de l’or, et s’est tantost refroidiez; et s’on le chaufe trop; si font au feu; et ensi i a assez d’empechement.	And when you heat the instrument with gold, you do not know if it is hot by its golden color, and it has been too cooled; and if you heat it too much, it melts; and then it has enough prevention.
Et por ce usons nos de cautere de feir que nos l’avons mues apparilliet a nostre oevre.	And that is why we use fire cauteries in our work, as we have mentioned before.
Or vos ai ordeneit cest chapitre des lou chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que li voie soit plus legiere a trover.	Or if you have ordered this chapter of the little joints, because it is easier to find.
dou cautere olivaire	olive cauteries
Cist cauteres vaut a moistor et a froidor sus lou cerveil, et en i a dous c’on fait par la cause d’une maladie qui est apelee «soda», et par la cause de maintes humors qui dessendent dou chief as eulz, et as oreilles, et por multitude de songes et dolor de dens et dolor de gorge, et meismement a toutes maladies qui vienent de froidor si com paralisie et sode et apoplexie et semblans maladies.	This cauterization is useful for moisture and cold in the face, and it is done for the disease called "soda", and for many humors that descend from the head, and the ears, and numerous dreams and toothache and throat pain, and even for all diseases that come from cold, such as paralysis, stroke, apoplexy, and similar diseases.
Li forme de cest cautere si est que li malaides soit espurgiez par medicine solutive mondifiant le chief III nuis ou IIII, selonc ceu que li vertus et li eaige et li acostumance dou malaide le puet soffrir; et puis fai rere lou chief dou malaide.	The form of this cauterization is as follows: if the physician purges the patient with soluble medicine that modifies the third or fourth vessel, according to which virtues and age and custom of the physician the patient can endure; then repeat the dose of the physician.
Et puis le fai seoir croisiet entre tes mains, et mettre ses mains sor som peis; aprés met la racine de ta palme sus la racine de son neis entre ses II eulz; et lai ou venra tes dois moiens, si saigne d’enche puis eschaufe le cautere qui est apelé «olivare», de coi ci est li forme:	Then place the root of your palm between the root of his thumb and the second fingers; then if you have two hands, it will bleed, so squeeze the cautery called "olivare," which is formed as follows:
Et le met sor le leu signiet d’encre, et fai en dessendant et en estraignant ta main poc et poc en trestornant; puis lieve ta main isnelement, et rewarde le leu se tu vois l’os I sol petit; et se tu ne lou vois, si rencomence le cautere tant que tu voies l’os si com je lou t’ai dit; aprés pren I poc de seil, et met en awe et molle coton dedens, et met sor le leu, et li laisse III jors; aprés met sus cotun moilliet en burre; et laisse sus tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés cure la plaie de l’oignement qui est apelez «tetrafarmaçon», tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then place ink on the bone, and make it descend and tighten your hand repeatedly until you see the bone move slightly; then if you do not see it, continue the cauterization as long as you see the bone as I have told you; then take a piece of cloth, and make it soft and fine cotton, and place it on the bone, and let it lie for three hours; then put it in a warm bath; and leave it until the burn is healed; then apply the ointment called "tetrafarmaçon" to the wound as soon as it is healthy.
Et se dirent li ancien, que quant plus demoure overte li plaie, plus s’espurge; et por ce si aide mues.	And if the ancients had said that the more overgrown the wound is, the more it oozes; and this is why it helps.
Et dirent aucun de ces que on doit tant lassier le cautere que partie de l’os soit arse, et puis rese on ceu qui est ars de l’os, et soit curez.	And none of these say that the fire cautery should be so tight that part of the bone is cut, and then remove what is cut from the bone, and treat it.
Et dient li autre c’on doit le cautere tant lassier sus, et bouter si fort c’on abaite de l’os ausi large comme I vertoil que les femmes mettent en lor fusez por ceu que les humors issent mues hors; et doit on lassier la plaie longement overte; aprés le doit on curer et sodeir.	And they say that the fire cautery should be so tight that it presses on the bone as far as the width of the vessel that women put in their wounds because the humors escape outside; and it should be tightened for a long time over the wound; after that, it must be treated and sutured.
Et ces II manieres de cauteres ne me semblent mie estre bones dou tout en tout, fuers qu’en aucuns homes ou il ait voie de paor; et mues me semble que je lou doie laissier; car li chiés li est afoiblis par les solutions continuees de nature, si com nos le tesmoignons ens autres membres; et meisme quant li chiés dou malaide est foibles par nature, et li premiere semblance de cautere est plus salve et muedre por moi, et de celi use je oevre en donques emsamble salut.	1. These two methods of cauterization do not seem to be the best in general, although they may seem effective for some men or those who fear; it seems to me that I should leave them alone, as the heads of the bones are weakened by continuous natural solutions, as we have experienced in other parts; and even when the patient's bones are weak by nature, the first appearance of cauterization seems more salve and milder for me, and therefore I use it in this way.
de l’anciainne dolor dou chief	2. of ancient pain of the head
Quant en tout le chief vient dolor croniques, et dure longement, si doit user li malaides yeris et pilules qui sont apelees «cochie», et d’espurgement de chief et d’oiles et d’emplastres; et s’on li fait le cautere que nos avons devant dit, et il ne vaut.	3. When all the head is in chronic pain and lasts a long time, if one must use the drugs called "cochies" and pills, as well as purging of the head and oils and plasters; and if it is made with the cauterization we have mentioned before, and it does not work.
Pren warde se li chiés dou malade est de fort nature, et qu’il ne soit trop froit; adonques le cauterize desoz celui cautere un poc que nos avons dit desus.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Aprés fai cautere sus chescune corne dou chief jusc’a l’os, si com devant avons dit, et fai I cautere ou leu qui est apelez «vasselz»; et est I leus en coi on met ventouses; et alige ta main si que tu ne voises mie jusc’a l’os: li malaides sent trop plus grant dolor en cest cautere que as autres, et je em parlerai aillors; et covient que li cauteres des cornes soient plus subtis que cil dont on cautere la moieneteit dou chief, et c’est li forme:	After making the cauterization at each cornea of the shoulder, as we have described, and then making a cauterization on the bone that is called "vassals"; and these are the ones that are put into a vacuum; and hold your hand so that you do not see the bone: the patient feels too much pain in this cauterization than in others, and I will explain further; and it is necessary that the cauterizations of the corneas be more superficial than those made on the shoulder joint, and this is the form:

Quant en une partie dou chief vient dolor sodaine, et est estendue li maladie jusc’a l’oil, et li chiés est espurgiez par medicines mondifians, et on a fait les autres cures que j’ai dit en la division des maladies, et tout ceu ne profite mie: adonques li fai cauteres selonc II manieres, c’est a savoir de medicine ague et de feir.	When sudden pain comes to one part of the fire cautery, and it spreads throughout the disease, and the head is purged with medicines modified, and the other treatments I mentioned in the division of diseases are made, and none of this helps: therefore, I made the cauterizations in two ways, that is, with medicinal heat and force.
Li cauteres de medicine ague si est que tu preignes une doce d’alz, et oste l’escorce et le recope I poc as II chiés, et puis fent la temple ou li dolor tient en teil maniere que tu puisses reponre la doce d’alz desoz le cuir; et quant elle sera reponuee si le lie et l’estraint bien et le laisse ensi XII houres; et puis le deslie et trait fuers la doce d’ail, et laisse la plaie ensi II jors ou III; puis met sus cotun plongiet en burre tant que porreture en isse.	If you apply medicinal heat and the wound odes and reopens in two hours, then make a temple with the head in such a way that you can place the dose of aloe back on; and when it is placed, if the lip and the ear are well drawn and left for twelve hours; then remove the dose of aloe and leave the wound for two or three days; then put the cut under pressure as much as possible.
Aprés le cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez; et se tu vues si fai ceu d’aucunes medicines comburans que j’ai escrites ou dozime traitier des medicines comburans.	After the treatment of inflammation as soon as it is healthy; and if you see that there are no such medicines that I have written or treated with other remedies for such medicines.
Li cautere de fer si est selonc ceste meniere.	The iron burn if it follows this manner.

Se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere encor une fois, et autre se tu en as mestier, et le laisse III jors; aprés i met sus coton moilliet en burre, et lou cure de l’oignement desiccatif tant qu’il soit sanez, et se XL jors passent qu’il ne soit sanez, si met sus medicine ague corrosive tant que li os soit descovers; et lou reis selonc ceu que il venrait en son chapistre.	If not, continue the cauterization once more, and if you have experience, and let it lie for three days; then place cotton wool on the bride, and apply the desiccative ointment as long as it is dry, and when forty days have passed and it is dry, if apply an ague corrosive medicine so that the bone is exposed; and follow according to what comes in your chapter.
Et i a une maniere de cautere de fistule que aucun des anciens dirent.	And there is a way of cauterizing fistulas that no ancient one has ever said.
Entens a fistule, et fens le leu; aprés met en la fendure I camahan subtil de coi ci est li forme:	Understands the fistula, and then put in the fire cautery the thinnest part of the skin; afterwards, make a small cut in the place where it is, and you will find the form.
et i font a la quantiteit d’une .З. de plonc; et tien ta main ou camahan fermement, et ne se mueve li malaides nes point, que li plons fondus ne corre a son oil; et covient c’on mette sus l’oil a malaide coton moilliet en abin d’uefz ou en awe: li plonc si art lou leu de fistule, et lou saine per mervillouse saniteit.	And they make it to the thickness of a small dot; and hold your hand firmly on the fire cautery, and do not move the patient until the dots have melted and stopped moving, and it is necessary to put the oil on the fine cotton cloth or in a swab: the dot if it is close to the fistula, and the healthy part of the skin.
Et se li fistule est sanee per le cautere que nos avons dit, c’est boin.	If the fistula is healed by the fire cautery we have described, it is good.
Se ce non, si covient aministrer pertus au neif, et ramener la fistule au cors dou neif selonc ceu qu’il covient en som propre leu.	If not, then the physician should administer an enema to the newborn, and return the fistula to its proper place according to what is best for the child's own health.
des crevaices en levres	cracks in the lips
Mout de fois avienent crevaices en levres que sont apelees «poil», et meismement en levres des enfans.	Many times cracks in the lips are called "cracks" and the same in children's lips.
Quant tu cures ces crevaices de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et li cure ne profite, adonques eschaufe I petit cautere cultellaire selonc ceste forme:	When you treat these cracks according to what we have described in divisions, and the treatment does not help, then use a small fire cautery according to this form:
Et le met hastanment en celles crevaices tant qu’il viegne jusc’a font; aprés cure le leu de cerote tant qu’il soit sanez.	And place the joint in those cracks as much as it can go; after, heal the limb with care until it is healthy.
de l’aposteme de la goule	of the abscess of the groin
Quant apostume vient en la racine de la goule ou en l’uve, ou ou palais, ou as racines des dens, aprés fait porriture et ront et est enveillis et devient fistule; et tu le cures si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie: adonques covient il que tu aies I cautere selonc la quantiteit de la fistule; aprés le bote ou pertus de la fistule, et tien ta main tant que li fer chaus viegne au font de li, et ou derrien leu; et fai ensi une fois ou II, aprés le cure de ce que nos avons dit en cures, tant qu’il soit sanez; et s’il est curez ensi, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si covient descovrir le leu et oster l’os corrumput, selonc ceu que vos le troverez en son chapistre.	When an abscess forms in the groin or urethra, or in the roots of the teeth, and it becomes inflamed and forms a fistule; and you treat it as we have said in divisions, and it does not heal well: then it is necessary that you cauterize according to the size of the fistule; after the bore or puncture of the fistule, and hold your hand until the fire reaches the source of the fistule, and if it goes in; and make once or twice, after the cure of what we have said in the cures, as soon as it is healthy; and if it is cured once or twice, it is good; and if not, then it is necessary to reveal the leu and open the corrupted bone, according to what you will find in its chapter.
dou movement des dens	The first sentence to translate is: "Ou cautere
Quant les gencives sont mollifies par moistor et les dens muevent, et tu le cures per medicines et ceu ne vaut, adonc met le chief dou malaide en ton sain; aprés eschaufe le cautere dont li forme venra ci aprés en teil maniere que tu mettes une cainne sor le dent; et met dedens le cautere chaut hastanment, et tien tant ta main que li malaides sente la chalor venant a la racine dou dent; aprés lieve ta main et rencomence le cautere selonc ta volenteit; aprés emplisse li malaides sa bouche d’awe salee, et la teigne une houre et raiche fuers.	When the gums are softened by moisture and the teeth move, and you treat them with medicine and it does not work, then place the hard tooth in your mouth; after that wash the cauterization that came from it in this way that you put a nail under the tooth; and remove the teeth from the cauterization with great force, and hold your hand tightly on the patient's jaw so that the patient feels the pain coming from the root of the tooth; then gently release your hand and continue the cauterization according to your will; then fill the patient's mouth with wet earth, and paint it once a day and rinse thoroughly.
Et en teil maniere li dens qui estoit movans si est confermez, et li gencive mollifie restrainte, et li moistors corrumpue sechie.	And in this way, the teeth that were moving are confirmed, and the genital area becomes soft and restrained, and the moisture is dried out.
de la dolor des dens	of the pain of the teeth
Quant dolor de dens vient por froidor, ou il i a froidor ou veir, et les cures de medicine ne valent, adonc i ait mestier de cautere selonc II manieres: et cautere de burre et cautere de feu.	When the pain of the teeth comes from cold, or it is cold, and the remedies of medicine do not help, then it has to be treated in two ways: either by cauterization with a burr or by fire cauterization.
Cautere de burre si est telz que tu preignes burre de vaiche, et le bout en une cuillier de fer ou d’arain; aprés pren coton et envolope sus la pointe d’une tente, et la moille en burre bulit, et met sus le dent dolant hastanment et tien tant qu’il soit refroidiez; et ensi fai sovent tant que sa vertus viegne a la racine de la dent, et se tu vues si moille laine et coton en burre froit, et met sus le dent doillant, et met sus I fer chaut tant que li feus viegne au chevement dou dent.	Cauterization with a burr if it is such that you have to use a woolen burr from a sheep, and the end in a iron or copper cup; then take cotton and wrap it around the point of a needle, and make the tooth bleed slowly and hold it until it is cold; and often I do this as long as the virtue of the root of the tooth lives, and if you see that the wool and cotton are burning in cauterization, and put on the tooth that is sore, and put on iron hot as much as the flesh lives at the end of the tooth.
Li cauteres ensamble feu si est telz que tu preignes uns cainne de fer ou d’arain, et soit grosse si que li feus ne viegne a la bouche dou malaide; aprés chaufe le cautere, de coi li forme venra ci aprés, et le met sus le dent et tien ta main tant que li cauteres soit refroidiez; fai ceu sovent, car li dolor sera ostee celui jor meisme ou l’endemain.	1. If the fire cautery is such that it burns like a red-hot iron or copper, and is large enough to reach the mouth of the patient; then heat the cautery, and after forming it, place it on the tooth and hold your hand until the cautery is cool. Do this often, as the pain will be less for you or the next day.
Et covient que li malaides emplisse sa bouche de boin burre en l’empressement de cel cautere, et puis le raiche fuer; et c’est li forme dou cautere:	2. And it is necessary that the patient fills their mouth with hot blood in the pressure of this cautery, and then it becomes redder; and this is the shape of the cautery:
Et fai cautere dou queil chief que tu voudras, et selonc ceu que tu as pooir; et c’est li forme de la caine:	I perform the burn as you desire, according to what you can bear; this is the form of the cauterization:
des scrophules	of scrofuly
Quant les scrophules sont de fleume et de moistors froides, et ne sont obeissans a digestion par medicines, adonques eschaufe le cautere cheveit de coi ci aprés vient li forme, et ait II aovertures por les fumees a issir au cautere de l’autre partie; et met le cautere chaut sus l’apostume une fois, ou II se mestier est, tant qu’il viegne au font de l’apostume; et se li apostume est petis si met cautere selonc la quantiteit de l’apostume, et le laisse ensi III jors; et met sus coton moilliet em burre tant que li arsure soit ostee; aprés cure le leu d’oignemens et de tentes tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the scrofuly is wet and cold, and does not respond to digestion by medicines, then wash the cauterization tool with water after it comes out of the form, and make two openings for the fumes to escape from the cauterization on the other side; and put the cauterization tool on the abscess as soon as it is ready, or as it should be, until the abscess pus comes out; and if the abscess is small, then use the cauterization according to the amount of pus, and leave it for three days; and put cotton on it as soon as the burn is healed, and treat the wound with ointments and poultices until it is healthy.
Li forme de la cainne:	The form of the chain:
Quant les moistors vainquent sus les chenals dou pormon, et meismement quant ce vient de froide complexion, adonc covient que li malaides soit voidiez premiers par medicines solutives; aprés li fai cautere a la racine de la gorge, et te garde que tu ne venir mie jusc’a la gorge, et n’ardre dou keur mais c’un poc.	When moisture enters the channels, and even when it comes from a cold complexion, it is necessary that the patient be treated with soluble medicines first; after that, the fire cautery is applied to the root of the throat, and you should not go too far into the throat, and do not burn more than a little.
Aprés li fai I autre cautere a la jointure dou col au chief de l’espinee, et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» de coi nos avons la forme devant; et cure le leu si com nos avons devant dit tant qu’il soit sanez.	After that, I perform another cautery at the junction of the collarbone and the head of the spine, and it is called the "clavicle" in our language; and treat the shoulder as we have described until it is healthy.
de la toust	Of the entire
Quant tous et maladie de pormon sont de moistors froides, et li malaides nen ait fievre ne sechor, et est li maladie anciaine, se li fai ij cauteres sus la forcele en leus vuis; et I autre cautere emmi le pis entre II mameles; et soit li cauteres qui est apelez «clavile» selonc la forme qui est devant dite.	When all the symptoms of the disease are cold and moist, and the patient has no fever or thirst, and it is an old disease, then make cauteries on the strong parts in the body; and the other cauterization is between the two ears; and that which is called "clavicle" according to the form mentioned before.
Et se tu vues, fai cautere en poignant a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins» de coi li forme est ci devant en la maladie des oreilles; et soient li poins jusc’a XXX, ou enqui entor.	And if you see, make cauterization by pricking at the entire cauterization which is called "points" according to the form mentioned before in the disease of the ears; and let the points be as many as XXX, or fewer.
Aprés cure le leu selonc ceu qui est devant dit, et soit li cauteres a III rains selonc ceste forme:	After the shoulder is healed according to what was said earlier, and this cauterization is done in three rains according to this form:
Et por ceu sont li cautere plus legier, por ceu que tu en fais III a cop.	And because they are lighter cauterizations, because you do them in three in a row.
de la dislocation de l’ajutoire	of the shoulder dislocation.
Quant li chiés de l’ajutoire est desaloiez par cause de moistor, et on le remet a leu, et il n’i puet demorer ains revient adés et desalue par petit movement qui avient, si com nos avons esproveit, adonques covient il que tu ramoinnes la dislocation premierement.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.

Et aucune fois est ajostez sus ce I nerf por coi il i a VIII cauteres.	And never is adjusted on this nerve because it has eight cauterizations.
Aprés met sus le cautere porrelz broiez avec seil; aprés fai reposer le malaide, et ne soit meus li membres par lonc tens tant qu’il soit bien confortez.	After you put the cauterization iron on the nerve with silk, and after the patient rests, and do not hurt the limbs by long tension as long as they are well comforted.
Et s’il est desaloiez desus, liquelz chose avient poc, adonques fait cautere sus l’epaisse dou cautere clavile, ou mout de cauteres en poignant.	If it is dislocated, something comes out quickly, so a cauterization is made on the thickest part of the cauterization clavicle, or from the point where the cauterizations are made.
Car li jointure est refermee, et est ostee li moistor et est sanez li malaides.	For the joint is closed, and it is relieved of moisture and becomes healthy.
Quant en l’estomac vienent froidures et mout de moistors tant qu’il l’estraient a sa complexion, et sont multipliet li catharre a lui, et es manieres de cures acostumees et il ne profite mie, adonc covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son dos, et estende ses jambes et ses mains.	When the stomach comes cold and wet as it is drawn to its complexion, and the catharsis is multiplied on it, and the customary treatments are applied, and it does not benefit, then the patient must have the abdomen soaked with water, extend his legs and hands.

For this reason, I made three cauterizations on the calf of the foot due to the quantity of a dose, at all the cauterization points, and two cauterizations on the costals as much as the cauterizations appear at three angles, and they should be spaced apart between one and another so that they are not joined together as they grow; and they should be the cauterizations if they point to the two parts of the knee, and the figure of the cauterizations should be according to this form in harmony.
Et se tu vues cauterize d’un grant cautere enmi l’estomac selonc ceste forme; et celui qui avra paour de cest cautere, cauterize en poignant et seigne sus l’estomac i. point selonc la quantiteit que tu vues d’enche; puis le cauterize a tot le cautere qui est apelez «poins».	2. And if you see cauterized on the stomach according to this form; and the one who suffers from this cauterization, cauterizes by touching and pressing on the stomach at the point according to what you see; then cauterize all the points that are called "points".
Aprés le cure de la cure que nos avons eut devant, tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the cure we had before, as long as it is healthy.
Quant au foie vient dolor de froit et de moistor et de grosse ventositeit, tant qu’il est fuer mis de sa complexion natureil per les superfluitez; et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne li profite mie, si covient que li malaides soit sovinez sus son haitereil; et signe d’enche III cauteres selonc ceste forme et ceste figure et ceste quantiteit sus lou foie, defuer les ypocondres, lai ou li coutes de l’ome vient; et ait d’espaice entre chaicun cautere la groissece d’un doi; et soient li cautere dou lonc dou cors, et ne presser mie mout ta main a tot le cautere; et soit arse tant soulement li moitiez dou keur, et soit li malaides drois sus ses piez; et s’il ne peut, si soit gisans, et estende ses jambes, et lieve ses brais; et c’est li forme:	When the liver causes pain and moisture and large ventosity, as long as it is properly placed in its natural complexion due to superfluities; and the patient is treated as we have said in divisions, and he does not benefit from it if he becomes angry with his hateful one; and sign of encephalitis according to this form and figure and quantity on the liver, defend the epigastrium, either the cost of the throat comes; and let there be space between each cauterization of a grotesque of a doe; and be the cautery long and not too close to the body; and only half of the moisture should be used on each cautery; and the patient should hold his breath tightly; and if it cannot, if it is crooked, and extends his legs, and leans his arms; and this is the form:
Et se ta volentez est, si cauterize ces cauteres dou cutellaire, se tu es subtilz et saiges en l’art, et te warde que tu n’ardes mie tout le keur, car tu feroies sechier tout le cors; et qu’il ne viegne jusc’a boueil, car li keurs est mout subtilz lai endroit, et lou saiches por voir.	And if your will is so, to cauterize these sharp cautery, be you subtle and gentle in the art, and have courage that you do not burn all of it, for you fear to dry the whole body; and that it does not become muddy, because the hair is very delicate in every place, and you see it for the sauce.
Quant il a apostume au foie, et tu vues savoir s’il est en la char dou foie ou en la toile: s’il est en la char, se sent li malaides dolor ne mie trop fort; et s’il est en la toile, si sent dolor forsenee. Et cauterize I cautere tant que li keurs soit ars, et viegne jusc’a syphac, tant que li porreture soit toute fuers; aprés la cure selonc la cure des essues tant qu’il soit sanez; et ne covient mie que de cest cautere use nuls fuers que cil qui ait estudieit longement en l’art de medicine, et par cui mains cestes maladies ont corrut aucune fois. Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Indeed, it is not easy to overcome, and I believe it is best to leave it alone.
dou cautere de pleuresin	Dou cauterization of plasters
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere: pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois; et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe; et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc; et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	The ancients said that one must make of plasters, and in this way: take an aristolochia root long, the longest you can find, and let it be dry, and as large and long as your fingers; and put it in oil, and take it to the fire, and cauterize I cautere between the force and the col, and II petis cauteres a pouch descending in the part which is desoz la barbe; and II cauteres between the fifth coste and the sixth, declining derrier a pouch; and I cautere emmi the pis, and I autre sus l'estomac, and I entre II espaules, and II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules; and do not press too hard with your hand, as you would smell.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme; et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	And no ancient said that any man uses a fire cautery like the scalpel, and they thrust it between the ribs, as soon as it reaches the abscess; and then there is great pain, as we have said in the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this case, there is pain or the patient dies now, or a fistula comes which cannot be saved.
de la mice	of the mouse.

de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not good for dropsy, for it is done in the way called "ascites".
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis; et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur. de l’enfleure des piez	of the enflaming of the wounds.
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire; et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner. de plaie mal curee	Of a wound that was not properly treated

Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés. de la dolor dou dos	Of the pain of the back

de la dolor des jointes	to relieve the pain of the joints.
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere: fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	When pain in the joints occurs due to swelling that spreads to all parts of the body, and when the pain comes from the foot, which is called "gout" properly, and when it is of a cold cause and medicines do not cure it, then it can be cured by cauterization in this way: make the joints dry with cauterization around the affected joint, and use olive oil according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	If it is desired that you touch the face with long and even hair, then the fire cautery is applied to the entire cautery as claimed "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire; et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	If the pain comes to the groin and other joints, and this happens many times, then the fire cautery is applied to each groin III cauteries or IV of each part, on the entire olive cautery; and if you have more skill, but do not hold your hand as long as the pain allows.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	If the pain descends to the groin and back, then apply the cautery we have mentioned in this chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes; et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main; et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	When the pain is in the hands, if there is no pain after a point on the flesh of II lines; and if there remains no pain, then make points at each joint and on the hair of the hand; and if the pain comes as costals or espaules, cauterize each part, and govern the patient's behavior with medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make good governance and purge the filth, then he will be healthy in the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the face
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor; et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre; aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors; puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	When the rupture comes in angles, and the wounds hang down as threads and it is new, then it happens that when you see to heal it, it does not come from the belly; and it uses things that make the belly soft, if it comes out of the belly; then make it lie on your back between your hands, and command it to lick its own tail as much as it can, and touch it to your two hands, and sign with a thumb that it is closed at the bone of the dry part, and all signs that are like the half of a circle at the corners of the wounds; then shave the cauterization of the form:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as it is white and feels cold.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu; et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier; et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains; puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os; et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere; que tu ne le brulasses; et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	Then mash the dough with your hands; and the baker signs his hand to make sure they don't return; and work well on the thighs of the patient, and put the cauterization sign on all the hand, and hold it right and hold it as long as you touch the bone, and if you don't touch the bone the first time, then continue another time until you reach the bone; and be gentle so that the dough doesn't rise when you make the cauterization sign, that you don't burn it; and so that the bread doesn't burn, or other food.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And you question whether when you do not come to the bone at the cauterization, your efforts are worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure; aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee; aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee; et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	It is necessary that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the size of the bone, and also great for adults; after three days, cure the foot of the cauterization as much as the burn is healed; after the cure of other ointments as long as it is healthy, and give him salves to his back for forty days as long as the wound is well-sored; and it is necessary that his hair be combed far away, so that the dregs do not come out when he goes to bed.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors; et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire; et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	And after forty years, when he wishes to rise, he should make a well-made girdle for himself, and every fourteen days; and let him rest, so that he works quickly and is not overly full of drink and food, and is too hot; and when he teaches this lesson, it is completely healthy.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will say this after the care of cutting in his chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the abdomen
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur; aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit; et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	When ruptures occur in other abdomens and are known, and you see that they are not increasing, then he should re-cauterize according to the quantity, and so is the third part of the keur; after the cure as we have said; and none of the ancients have said that it should be cauterized at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	The first line translates to: "But sign the leg and make a line for the width of the fracture, and another for the depth, and hold your hand on all the cauterizing claw.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	The second line translates to: "But the first cauterizations are more gentle and milder.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	The third line translates to: "with less pain in any limb.
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	The fourth line translates to: "When pain comes from any part of the body, whether from chill or wound, and this pain lasts long, and medicine does not help, then it is necessary to cauterize at the point called 'points', and to cauterize according to the length of the limb and its thickness, its flexibility, its strength, and its location of knots and its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien; se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	If the patient is healthy after the first fire cautery, that is good; if not, restart another fire cautery on the same member, as it is customary for the patient to die at the member that is being cauterized, because it is necessary to perform the cauteries until the patient is healthy.
de meselerie	of mollities
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The mollities are helped once by cauterization, and at the same time, the disease that comes from the putrefaction of flesh and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief: I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous; et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel; et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir; et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	Can you see the cauterization, before the disease is at its beginning, and when it is cured according to what we said in the division, and does not tire or become dull, and you doubt that corruption will spoil all the patient, therefore I perform the cauterizations on the head: I cut off the head, and the other on the forehead at the end of the jaws; and they touch the corners, and the backside to the hilt; and it lasts as long as your hand holds the cauterization, and as long as the discharges issue forth so that the vapors of the large humors may issue forth; and I cauterize on the nails according to what is before.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse; et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules; et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains; et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler; et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	When the wound is widespread and clearly visible; if it comes to it, that you cauterize with these cauteries that we have mentioned or chief, and the cauterization in some places, and the cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and the cauterizations on the spine of the back, and the crupieries and other wrists, and the shoulders, and the tendons of the ankles, and all the joints of the hands and feet, and the fissures of the hands; and you wear bandages that are below the knees, which do not burn, and never made a cauterization on the bone of the thumb, and the other on the stomach bone, and the other on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite; et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	When the more you do of cauterization, the more help it gives, and it benefits him; and advise that the surgeon does not feel pain in cauterization if it is as healthy as he thinks, because the heart is already corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it should be great and small according to the members and joints, according to what you will find in ways of iron.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After curing the dough with flour and honey and other remedies as long as it is healthy.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre; et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur; puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the wound comes in any member and is cured by drugs and oils and plasters, and it is not healthy, then the cauterization is done on the member according to its size and smallness; and if the cauterization enters into the spare part of the knee; then the treatment of ointments as long as it is healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure; et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	For no time is it done that the cauterization is made on the hand, arm, and back, at the end of the nerve that makes the member mute, and if it is not pierced, it does not enter; and all this is done without disturbing anything if one knows the members and the movements of the muscles in the body.
de albaras	of barbs
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color; puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie; et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	When the disease called "albaras" is awakened, and the art of medicine does not help, then it is cauterized with a cautery, according to the quantity of the blister's size, as long as the member is pierced and remains colorless; then the treatment of flour and lentils with olive oil and plantain flakes, and sand of colon and sand of alendron, of each part; and all are assembled, and bound with a bandage, and applied to the member as long as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of syphilis by burning
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When the sore appears at the beginning, and you see it stop, if the cauterization is done with the fire cautery that seems like a circle, then it should be completely around the entire sore.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre; et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois; et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	And the wise ones say that cauterization is done in the environment of the sore; and I think this is not bad, because I doubt that it will become ulcerated and corrupted, and I have always wanted this to happen once; and the most accurate thing is that it should be cauterized around, with the cautery called "circumcision," as we have said in the past.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	Of the inflammation that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens; et tu la vues haster de meurer: adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant; aprés le laisse ensi.	When someone has a disease called "adubelati", and it delays measuring either because of excessive production or due to the patient's old age (too many), and there is little blood, or due to tension; and you see it hurrying to measure: therefore, the cauterization is performed by touching several small cauteries; afterwards, it is left alone.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hurry to measure.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you see it hastening to measure, if the cauterization is too hot, then its form is like this:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And place your hand in the environment of this disease called "adubelati" as long as the cauterization is perceived, and be such cauterization that the patient feels it in a certain way that the course of the purulence is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment when it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	the cauterization by fire with iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease called "corrodens", and it is nothing but a rot of the member, as it rots the members as well as the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est; aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	If you see this disease in the shoulder that can be burned together with fire, then smooth the cauterizations clavicle as small and large as possible, according to where the disease is; after all are cauterized as much as possible, and nothing remains of it, that all that is corrupted is made bone.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it lie for three days, and put on the burned parts with oil as long as the scars from the fire are not healed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of burns caused by fire.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin; et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	And if after three days you do not see healthy char born, it is bad; and if it does, continue the cauterization on the parts that are still corrupted.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu; mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division: pren la quant tu en as mestier.	And this disease has never been cured by medical treatment in the place of fire cauterization; but all fire cauterization is greater help, and I have already said the cure of the medical treatment in the division: take what you have mastered.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	Of the porels that come to the pies
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it has happened that the feet are affected by a disease called "closed" according to our understanding, and it is a large thing that must be treated to heal the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the treatment of this disease is in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is known as fire cauterization, and hot water cauterization.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges; aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou; et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture; puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	Fire cauterization is when you heat the foot like a hot iron, and it is made of a bow with a hole in the middle as large as the nail can fit through, and has subtle margins; after it is placed on the nail, turn your hand around the nail as much as it goes to the end of the nail; and it leaves for three days until it starts to drip pus; then make a poultice of boiled, salted herbs, and place the poultice on all night, and the nail will be rooted and will be desrooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then care for the wound with ointment, applying it as soon as it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude; et est en teil maniere: pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues; et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine; et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre; puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	Then, if the wound becomes infected many times, and in hands and feet, it may be necessary to have a hot fire cautery; and it should be done in this way: take a copper or iron nail, or a feather, and put it on the nailhead and the nailstem, which is to cover wounds; then put the nail on so that it covers everything, then put a little hot water, and hold your hand well, and press your hand as you turn until the tip of the nail reaches the root of the nailhead, and then find the hot fire cavity halfway up the stem; then suffer the patient a little mordication of the hot fire for an hour; then remove it, and it will fall off at all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	I will perform another action as long as you are aware of all these in the course, then I will treat the wounds that are causing pain.
li cure dou trembler	I will cure it so it does not shake.
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee; et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire; si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	If the patient trembles due to cold, fever, or another cause, it is necessary that you perform four cauterizations or four on each spine; and one cauterization between each spine; and one at the stomach with olive oil; if the trembling stops and the health improves from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of pustules that have appeared.
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	No time has it appeared by deflowering the corpse, or pustules that come from large corrupted materials.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule: un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	If it is necessary to do a fire cauterization as soon as they appear, which is a subtle cauterization of gummy milk, or if the point is held in the heat, or of the cauterization of lentil shape, or by cautery of Aristotle's root.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez; mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	And no time is cauterization made at the beginning when they appear, according to this method, and it does not grow any warts in front, but it is disrupted by the superfluity that comes, and they are healthy; but it must be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	When the artery is tied off
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses; et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	Often there are great hemorrhages of blood from the artery that is tied off at the wound that comes to the paraduers, or at the incision of the abscess, or at the fire cautery of the member, and similar things; and it is a terrible thing to clean.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus; puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge; puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	And if there is nothing, if you must put your index finger on the wound of the vein, and hold it tight as long as it is not calmed by your finger, and does not cause pain; then put fire on the olive-wood cauteries more and less according to the size of the wound, and then I, or as much or as little as necessary to the vein and to the leu where the artery is tied, and put the cautery on this wound or where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery as long as it is not re-inflamed.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	If the patient feels pain when you tie the knot in the vein, and the cauterization ends, then quickly take another one that is hot.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez; et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide; et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit: ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc; et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	And continue to do this one after another until the nerve is no longer tense; and guard your hand so that you do not hurt the patient, and make sure that no other malice comes to the patient's limb; and be careful when you do not cut the artery, as it cannot be well treated immediately if the artery is large, unless it is one of the four methods we have mentioned: either by cauterization or by extraction if it is properly treated, or by gentle pulling with thread, or by medicines placed on it that can cause pain; and make sure to hold and stretch it.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	Whoever will strictly maintain the tightening of the cloth or the placing of things on it, or other similar things, should not profit from it unless.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne; et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez; et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	And if there is none and no remedy or medicine, then he should put his index on the wound of the vein as we have said, and firmly press until it is sore from the wound and the vein; and he should not move much, but often use cold water that is not too cold so that it does not freeze and become painful, and treat these things beforehand that are his skill in cauterization and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	Here comes the first sentence to translate:
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres; et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	1. We have told you in the first chapter about all diseases that require cauterization, either by fire or burning medicines, and their causes, effects, and forms of cauterizations; and I have made this chapter on the chief chief's own words, and I will go to this chapter by my own way because it is lighter to tell it.
